Summary",["$","$L10",null,{"id":"1-summary"}]]}],"\n",["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"“qwen tag”"}]," is one shared qwen-code agent that lives inside a chat channel — a DingTalk group first, Feishu second — and that any member of that channel summons by ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"@"}],"-mentioning it. Once summoned, it runs the full qwen-code agent loop (tools, file edits, shell, MCP) against a bound workspace, streams its work back into the channel as it goes, ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"remembers the channel across turns and restarts"}],", and can act ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"proactively or on a schedule"}]," without waiting to be asked. This mirrors the Claude Tag form factor — a single persistent multiplayer agent that is a ",["$","em",null,{"children":"resident"}]," of the room rather than a 1:1 DM bot — but it is built entirely on qwen-code’s existing channel adapter stack (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"qwen channel start"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"packages/channels/*"}],") and the ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"qwen serve"}]," daemon, not on a new hosted service."]}],"\n",["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":["The deliberate framing of this RFC is that ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"the reactive half of the form factor is largely already shipped, and the proactive/memory half is not."}]," The pieces that make a Claude-Tag-style ",["$","em",null,{"children":"reply"}]," agent hard — a long-running process that multiplexes sessions, an agent transport that preserves the one-prompt-per-session invariant, multiplayer session routing, per-channel access control, streaming card rendering, and durable session persistence — already exist and are exercised by the current channel adapters. What is ",["$","em",null,{"children":"missing"}]," is a well-bounded set of capabilities that turn a reactive reply-bot into a resident agent: sender attribution in shared sessions, a proactive/scheduled output path, per-room memory, and multiplayer governance. This RFC scopes that gap into ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"four build areas"}]," and specifies them across Phase 0–2."]}],"\n",["$","blockquote",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:border-gray-300 x:italic x:text-gray-700 x:dark:border-gray-700 x:dark:text-gray-400 x:border-s-2 x:ps-[1.5em]","children":["\n",["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":["Note on “80%”: earlier drafts framed this as “~80% shipped.” That figure is unverifiable and overstates the case — the entire proactive engine (Build Area 2) and per-room memory (Build Area 3) are net-new, and on DingTalk specifically there is ",["$","em",null,{"children":"no"}]," outbound-initiate path at all. We instead frame it as “the reactive path is built; the proactive and memory paths are not.”"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","h3",null,{"id":"a-topology-fact-that-constrains-the-entire-rfc","className":"x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-2xl","children":["A topology fact that constrains the entire RFC",["$","$L10",null,{"id":"a-topology-fact-that-constrains-the-entire-rfc"}]]}],"\n",["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":["There are ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"two distinct ways a channel adapter is wired to a qwen agent"}],", in ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"two different processes"}],", and conflating them is the single most common error in earlier drafts:"]}],"\n",["$","ul",null,{"className":"x:[:is(ol,ul)_&]:my-[.75em] x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:list-disc x:ms-[1.5em]","children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"qwen channel start <name>"}]," (the shipping path)."]}]," ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"start.ts"}]," constructs ",["$","strong",null,{"children":["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"new AcpBridge(bridgeOpts)"}]}]," (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"start.ts:213,268,356,435"}],"), and ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"AcpBridge.start()"}]," ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"spawns a child"}]," ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"node <cliEntryPath> --acp"}]," process (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"AcpBridge.ts:53-70"}],"), talking ACP over NDJSON on ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"stdio"}],". This child is a ",["$","em",null,{"children":"standalone agent"}],", not the ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"qwen serve"}]," HTTP daemon. In this topology there is ",["$","strong",null,{"children":["no HTTP daemon, no ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"/workspace/memory"}]," route, no ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"MultiClientPermissionMediator"}],", no ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"eventBus"}]," replay ring, and no daemon ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"promptQueue"}]]}]," — those all live in ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"packages/acp-bridge"}]," + ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"packages/cli/src/serve"}],", which ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"qwen channel start"}]," never instantiates. Prompt serialization here is done entirely ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"channel-side"}]," by ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"ChannelBase"}]," (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"activePrompts"}]," mutex at ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"ChannelBase.ts:356-391"}]," + ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"sessionQueues"}]," chain at ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":":394-470"}],") and by the child’s own ACP one-prompt-per-session invariant. ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"AcpBridge.requestPermission"}]," ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"auto-approves every tool call"}]," (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"AcpBridge.ts:108-118"}],")."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"qwen serve"}]," + ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"DaemonChannelBridge"}]," (daemon-hosted)."]}]," ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"DaemonChannelBridge"}]," (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"packages/channels/base/src/DaemonChannelBridge.ts"}],") is an in-process bridge whose ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"sessionFactory"}]," produces daemon ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"Session"}]," objects. This path runs channels inside the daemon and thereby inherits ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"acp-bridge"}],"’s FIFO ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"promptQueue"}]," (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"bridge.ts:232,2855,3082"}],"), ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"MultiClientPermissionMediator"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"eventBus"}],", and the HTTP routes. ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"autoReconnect"}]," only refetches on socket ",["$","em",null,{"children":"close"}]," (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"client.mjs:157-163"}],") — a stable long-lived socket holds a stale token past the ~2 h TTL, and any proactive send (and the existing emotion/media paths) silently fails once it expires.
